< Text>
BEST nail salon in Ridgecrest HANDS DOWN!!!

Okay so, I recently relocated out here because like most who come to the high desert, my husband is stationed on the China Lake military base.
Starting new all over, I set out on a MONTH LONG hunt for THE BEST OF THE BEST nail & hair enthusiasts in town. This included reading EVERY (and I mean EVERY SINGLE REVIEW) of nail/hair salons in this location.

Yesterday, was the VX9 Vampire Christmas party AND also, my first day at my new job! To honor these two special occasions, I really had my heart set on getting a fresh full acrylic mani! Still having yet to try out any salons post my review readings, I remembered luxury nails had some of the best reviews and most lovely pictures!
So, I took a leap of FAITH & set up an appointment an hour before I was scheduled to go in for training for my new job! and...

OH MY GOODNESS! THANK JESUS FOR THE ANGEL ON MY SHOULDER THAT GUIDED ME TO TAKE THAT LEAP!  I got there and NO JOKE, within 10 mins OR LESS I was in a chair being worked on! The BEST PART, for THE FIRST TIME in my whole life & experience with getting my nails done, NOT ONE PERSON urged me to change my mind of color, design, or shape!! NOT ONE person made me feel unwelcome or like their interests were solely driven by money.

I usually don't write reviews but what luxury nails did for me yesterday was beyond some of the most caring & courteous behavior I have EVER experienced at a nail salon. I was going to be a few minutes late on my FIRST DAY on the job because I made the mistake of not scheduling more ahead (The manicurist who worked on me was VERY thorough and dedicated to giving me the exact look I wanted, which of course lets be honest ladies, takes time!) . My husband paid & I expressed my concern about being a tad late & my manicurist so generously offered to let me come back anytime before closing or even the proceeding day so that they could finish! They were NOT about to let me be walking around with half ass looking nails and that to me, TRULY means something! That told me instantly, these people take PRIDE in their work! I came back after training & they were super caring & expressed genuine concern for how my day went & if I got there on a decently timely manner.

EVERYONE loved my nails at the Christmas party & I have not stopped receiving compliments ever since! I even got a complement just earlier today at Walmart & what I found AMAZING was the woman who complemented me INSTANTLY KNEW I had got them done at Luxury Nails! NEEDLESS TO SAY, I HIGHLY RECOMMEND & I think, wait, NO I KNOW, I've found my new spot! <3< /Text>

<text>I have went to freeway insurance in Moreno Valley for three years for my auto insurance needs. This year I wanted to add a vehicle to my existing policy. My existing payment for two vehicles was $169 a month and I remember paying close to $400 to start it up October of 2019. She told me that my next payment after adding the vehicle would be $264 and each month after $221. Reluctantly, I went to the store to finish up the process. When I spoke to Andrea (initially completed my policy last year), she told me it would be $100 service fee in additional to what Natasha told me. I felt that was not fair due to me being a current customer and doing all the foot work myself by phone for hours. She called over her manager and she offered to lower the fee to $50. I almost paid it but I left and decided to call the insurance company myself. National General re-instated my policy for the two vehicles and added the additional one for pennies. My next payment was $184 ($15 more than my monthly payment) on my regular date and each reoccurring monthly payment for the next 11 months is now $161, which is $8 less than it was with the two vehicles. Sometimes doing things yourself pays off. It did for me. This took less than ten minutes!!!! When you feel like your being ripped off, you probably are. <Review>Subway has nothing on Which Wich. The quality of breads, meats and ingredients offered here is far superior. I have to admit, for awhile I would have lunch during breaks in between classes next door at The Habit and did not have a desire to try Which Wich. My classmates would always get sandwiches here which always looked good, but I guess I am just more a fan of burgers. That all changed when they started offering Philly cheese-steak. Whatttt they have cheez wiz now???? Now I dont have to fly all the way to Philadelphia to eat at Pats or Genos to get my cheese-steak fix. I ordered a large sandwich which came with an abundance of meat, cheez wiz, provolone, onions and peppers. Downed the whole thing in 10 mins. The service here is great, the restaurant is clean. It can get busy at times, sometimes you have to wait  upwards of 15 mins to get your sandwich made, but the level of attention and quality is worth it.< /Review>< pics>

< Review>
So, this is not the typical place I would select if I just looked at the interior: If you didn't know, you would assume to be in a Dodgers fans' club house, with dark interior, multiple insignia, and endless screens. However, the food - typical by name - was in fact very good. What do you get: burgers - ha, no surprise! What did we really get apart from a decent beer: a very juicy and tasty Filet Burger, a Classic Burger, and a Turkey Burger, combined with Truffle Fries, Sweet Fries, followed by a charming Vanilla Bread Pudding with ice cream ... Again, for the food, I'd come back.< /Review>

< Text>
In the ever present rivalry between BWW and Wingstop, the wing-off is won and lost in the execution. There are a few ways that the chicken here could be improved.

The chicken could definitely be juicier. The meat was dry and stringy. Then they can afford to put a bit more sauce on the wings. I don't know how much money they are saving from the reduced quantity of sauce, but they are losing revenue on people choosing their rivals.

The most mind numbing part is the service. No one is available to ask for the check, or refills, or asking questions. You have sit and wait... and wait... and wait. Not fun. I don't know why I came here...</Text>

I come here purely to watch sports. Anywhere you sit there's a good view of the game or fight. I was here for the Rams/Chiefs game last night. They had it on about 70% of the screens, with the volume on in both rooms. Tall Modelo Especials were $5 during the game. I can't recommend the food here. The fries taste stale.
